  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_0a8cca91-e16a-41e1-a8d1-c5678a0860b3'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

He knows he was friends with Clary, and that he convinced the total goddess Isabelle Lightwood to go out with him…but he doesn’t know how. And when Clary and Isabelle look at hi</span>
  <span id="freeText7243397900012118604" style="display:none">Simon Lewis has been a human and a vampire, and now he is becoming a Shadowhunter. But the events of <i>City of Heavenly Fire</i> left him stripped of his memories, and Simon isn’t sure who he is anymore. He knows he was friends with Clary, and that he convinced the total goddess Isabelle Lightwood to go out with him…but he doesn’t know how. And when Clary and Isabelle look at him, expecting him to be a man he doesn’t remember…Simon can’t take it.<br /><br />So when the Shadowhunter Academy reopens, Simon throws himself into this new world of demon-hunting, determined to find himself again. His new self. Whomever this new Simon might be.<br /><br />But the Academy is a Shadowhunter institution, which means it has some problems. Like the fact that non-Shadowhunter students have to live in the basement. And that differences—like being a former vampire—are greatly looked down upon. At least Simon is trained in weaponry—even if it’s only from hours of playing D&amp;D.<br /><br />Join Simon on his journey to become a Shadowhunter, and learn about the Academy’s illustrious history along the way, through guest lecturers such as Jace Herondale, Tessa Gray, and Magnus Bane. These ten short stories give an epilogue to the Mortal Instruments series and provide glimpses of what’s in store in the Dark Artifices.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7243397900012118604" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>
</div>

Popular Answered Questions

<div id='communityQuestionsWithAnswers'>
<div class='communityQuestionAndAnswer'>
<div class='communityQuestion'>
<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/672117-i-know-these-came-out-in-ebook-form">I know these came out in ebook form originally, but since the bind-up is only coming out in November and Lady Midnight is out in March, which do I read first? This or Lady Midnight? Or does it not matter?</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>
<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_672117'><a id="like_count_community_question_672117" rel="nofollow" href="/rating/voters/672117?resource_type=CommunityQuestion"><span class="likesCount">3 likes</span></a>&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;<a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F28954137-tales-from-the-shadowhunter-academy">like</a></span>

</li>
<li class='footerItem communityQuestionTimestamp'>
<a href="/questions/672117-i-know-these-came-out-in-ebook-form">4 years ago</a>
</li>
<li class='footerItem communityQuestionPermalink'>
<a href="/questions/672117-i-know-these-came-out-in-ebook-form">See all 7 answers</a>
</li>
</ul>
</div>

<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/18169137-roger-brennand"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1362735616i/18169137._UX100_CR0,16,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/18169137-roger-brennand">Roger Brennand</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Yes ... and No ...<br/>It kind of depends how deep you want to go into your characters and storylines ... and backstories etc.<br/>Every Cassandra Clare Novel (<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Yes ... and No ...<br />It kind of depends how deep you want to go into your characters and storylines ... and backstories etc.<br />Every Cassandra Clare Novel (or Novella) is designed to be a "stand alone" story ... so, no you don't have to read anything gone before to pick up the 'gist' of what's going on. BUT ... in order to get the very best out of the story you're reading, understand certain references etc, then yes - it's a good idea to have read what has come before.<br /><br />I wouldn't stress though ... you can grab 'Tales' once it comes out in hard copy ... and then reread Lady Midnight with a whole new insight (just like a lot have us have done with The Mortal Instruments after The Bane Chronicles were released!) ... The beautiful thing about owning a book!<br /><br />Lady Midnight is awesome enough to keep you occupied anyway<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>
</div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2564114842" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9967077495417216670"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1539716242i/26459004._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>1.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2008644944' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Bones</a> ★★★<br/>2.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2373838717' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Ashes</a> ★★<br/>3.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2463489480' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Glass</a> ★★★<br/>1.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2465856942' rel='nofollow noopener'>Clockwork Angel</a> ★★★<br/>4.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2489169365' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Fallen Angels</a> ★<br/>2.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2518308849' rel='nofollow noopener'>Clockwork Prince</a> ★★★★<br/>5.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2526157370' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Lost Souls</a> ★★★★<br/>3.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2531117647' rel='nofollow noopener'>Clockwork Princess</a> ★★★★★<br/>6.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2544728646' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Heavenly Fire</a> ★★★★★<br/>*.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2552335362' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Bane Chronicles</a> ★★★<br/><br/>With the way that <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2544728646' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Heavenly Fire</a> ended, I couldn’t wait to get my hands on <i>Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy</i>! I thought this was going to be everything, but sadly I was a little let down. I mean, a few of the stories in here are the best I’v</span>
  <span id="freeText9967077495417216670" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1539716242i/26459004._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>1.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2008644944" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Bones</a> ★★★<br>2.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2373838717" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Ashes</a> ★★<br>3.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2463489480" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Glass</a> ★★★<br>1.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2465856942" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Angel</a> ★★★<br>4.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2489169365" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Fallen Angels</a> ★<br>2.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2518308849" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Prince</a> ★★★★<br>5.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2526157370" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Lost Souls</a> ★★★★<br>3.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2531117647" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Princess</a> ★★★★★<br>6.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2544728646" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Heavenly Fire</a> ★★★★★<br>*.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2552335362" rel="nofollow noopener">The Bane Chronicles</a> ★★★<br><br>With the way that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2544728646" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Heavenly Fire</a> ended, I couldn’t wait to get my hands on <i>Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy</i>! I thought this was going to be everything, but sadly I was a little let down. I mean, a few of the stories in here are the best I’ve read from this universe ( <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2568679788" rel="nofollow noopener">Bitter of Tongue</a> &amp; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2570590469" rel="nofollow noopener">Born to Endless Night</a>) but most just felt boring to me, if I’m being honest. I know that sounds horrible, but I just feel a little let down, I guess. <br><br>This anthology follows Simon during his time in the academy that spans two years and I’m assuming catches the reader up to date for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2570227019" rel="nofollow noopener">Lady Midnight</a>. But we also get to see so many other beloved characters, both from past and present. But most importantly, we get to see Simon be the person who he wants to be, after so much was taken from him in The Mortal Instruments. <br><br>Simon is my second favorite Shadowhunter character. He is Jewish, he is nerdy, he is funny, he is a good friend, he is selfless, and he is so very easy to love. And he really has been through so damn much in his life; none of it he asked for but was just thrust upon him. Him and Izzy are also my favorite ship, even though I think she was a little questionable during some of these stories, too. I feel like a lot of people couldn’t empathize with everything that Simon was struggling with, and it just made me sad every single time. <br><br>Overall, I had a lot of fun reading this, but again I did think that most of the stories were a little lackluster and left a lot to be desired. Yet, I still had a lot of fun while reading this! But I am going to break down each short story with my thoughts, opinions, and individual star rating!<br><br>➽ <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2565468854" rel="nofollow noopener">Welcome to Shadowhunter Academy</a>
</b> - ★★<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He waved good-bye to all these people he barely knew and somehow loved anyway, and he hoped they could not tell how relieved he was to be going.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Yikes, we aren’t off to a good start. Okay, this anthology picks up right after the events of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2544728646" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Heavenly Fire</a>, but Simon still doesn’t remember everything that happened, but he is now enrolled at the New York Institute. We get to meet so many new students, since the Shadowhunter world is in desperate need to replenish their fighters! I already love George. I already hate Jon. I will say that at first, I was so happy with Izzy’s declaration of love for Simon, but the more and more I kept thinking about it, I kept realizing that I was showing double standards, because if a dude would have done that to a girl I would have really disliked it. I will say that I always appreciated that Simon is the *nerdy one* and Izzy is the *popular one* and how Cassie Clare really plays that opposite trope up to perfection, but Izzy’s speech was a little too much even for me. I want good angst, not forced angst. <br><br>➽ <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2565470423" rel="nofollow noopener">The Lost Herondale</a>
</b> - ★★★<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“We all have our own story of the Dark War. All of us lost something. Some of us lost everything.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>We get to see Simon and twenty of his classmates try and kill their first law breaking Downworlder, but it happens to be a vampire that new Simon before his memories were lost. We get to learn a story about Tobias Herondale, the younger brother of Will, and it is heartbreaking. This story really shows how there are always two sides to a story, and in this case three. I love Catarina so very much, and I really enjoyed the message about how you have to be the person you want to be, and to always listen to your heart. Also, Jon is such a little shit. Also, also, I’m not here for the Izzy pity party, especially with everything Simon has had to go through since he got thrust into this world even though he never asked for any of it. Also, also, also there is an uncharted Herondale line? Lord, help us all. <br><br>➽ <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2566665651" rel="nofollow noopener">The Whitechapel Fiend</a>
</b> - ★★★★<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The trick to falling is not to fall…”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Oh, my word, there was a lot to like about this one! Not only do we get to see Jace training Shadowhunter kids to jump out of trees, we also get to see Tessa, Will, and Jem solving… get ready for it… the Jack the Ripper murders in 1888 London! Like, I was for sure not expecting to wake up and read that today! But what a gift! <br><br>➽ <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2566666942" rel="nofollow noopener">Nothing but Shadows</a>
</b> - ★★★★<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“James Herondale was the son of angels and demons,” she said softly. “He was always fated to walk a difficult and painful path, to drink bitter water with sweet, to tread where there were thorns as well as flowers. Nobody could save him from that. People did try.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>My favorite thing about the Shadowhunter world? Seeing all these family trees! Like, it is a little hard to keep straight, especially with the Lightwoods, but it just gives me all the warm and fuzzies. Also, seeing James Herondale and Matthew Fairchild become friends gave me all the feels. Again, if you couldn’t tell by my review of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2552335362" rel="nofollow noopener">The Bane Chronicles</a>! I need <i>The Last Hours</i> immediately! But I also love the growing friendship between George and Simon, too! Also, that letter he wrote to Izzy? Ah, my heart! <br><br>➽ <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2567718468" rel="nofollow noopener">The Evil We Love</a>
</b> - ★★<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He just knew, on a level beneath reason and memory, that some part of him belonged with Isabelle.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br>Easily one of my least favorite short stories set in the Shadowhunter world. Simon and still struggling with his memories, and Izzy is being unnecessarily cruel about it, in my opinion. Then her dad, Robert Lightwood (yuck), and her come to teach the new academy kids an important lesion, while Izzy just goes out of her way to try to lash out and hurt Simon constantly. And Robert gives the kids a flashback to 1984 when Valentine is starting to show his true intentions, but people choose to follow him anyway, for many different reasons. <b>TW</b> for murder, torture, and homophobia. <br><br>➽ <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2567718898" rel="nofollow noopener">Pale Kings and Princes</a>
</b> - ★★★★★<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“This is how a faerie loves: with a gift.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Easily one of my favorite short stories set in the Shadowhunter world. Summer is over, and Simon is back at the academy for his second year! But Helen Blackthorn and Aline Penhallow mean more to me than 99% of the characters I’ve spent all of 2018 reading about nonstop. But, can we please kill off professor Mayhew already? Like, I’m begging. What an insufferable asshole. But the Institute brings Helen to force her to tell the story of her half fae parentage, while humiliating and belittling her constantly. But she does it so that she can marry the love of her life, who has stuck by her side even when she was exiled to a cold island just because of how she was born. But the reason I loved this story so much was because the true story that even Helen doesn’t know about her mother and Faerie. Like, it was perfect. Everything I’ve ever wanted. Oh, and Simon and Izzy finally make up, but it for sure didn’t mean as much to me, because the last story was so damn painful to read! Like, can Helen and Mark just have their own anthology? Please. I loved this.<br><br>➽ <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2568679788" rel="nofollow noopener">Bitter of Tongue</a>
</b> - ★★★★★<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I got distracted making out with a boy, and then locked up by a goblin”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Is anyone really surprised that I loved the story about a sapphic marriage between a fae girl and an Asian girl? I have loved these two since their introduction and… their ceremony was everything! Also, this was so amazing because we got to see more of the fae court! Seriously, all I want is more of Mark and Kieran and the Hunt! Please, Cassie Clare, I’m begging you! I honestly just think the Blackthorns are my favorite family. Plus, seeing Izzy and Mark both try to save Simon in very different ways was pretty perfect. This is also the first story that made me feel like Sizzy was back, and it warmed my heart and made me so excited for the final three stories!<br><br>➽ <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2568680398" rel="nofollow noopener">The Fiery Trial</a>
</b> - ★★★<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“True parabatai are linked long before the ceremony takes place.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>This one I feel really on the fence about. Like, drugging people, even with good intentions, isn’t cool. Basically, this is the parabatai short story! We get to see Julie and Beatriz decide to become parabatai. We get to see Emma and Julian become parabatai. And then we get to see Simon and Clary discuss if they want to be parabatai. And… I thought I would like it more than I did. First off, Maureen is the character in this entire Shadowhunter universe that makes me the saddest. Then, add in the drugging situation. Lastly, the feeling weirdness because you know that Emma and Julian are obviously going to eventually have a forbidden romance (even though they are only fourteen in this… yikes!) I don’t know, I am excited to see Simon and Clary become parabatai, but this story wasn’t that great itself.<br><br>➽ <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2570590469" rel="nofollow noopener">Born to Endless Night</a>
</b> - ★★★★★<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Obviously you would call them Malec,” said Beatriz. “Are you stupid, Simon?”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Best Shadowhunter story ever! EVER! Seriously, this was probably my favorite thing in all of Shadowhunter history. Besides absolutely loving Magnus with everything that I am, seeing him be able to achieve things he never thought possible, even with his immortal life, is just so damn pure and wonderful. I also really appreciated Catarina and Lily in this story, too. Even though I really am dying to know everything about Tobias Herondale’s baby and the past. But yeah, this story was pure joy to read, and really just celebrate the love and honor for family; both blood and found.<br><br>➽ <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2570592926" rel="nofollow noopener">Angels Twice Descending</a>
</b> - ★★★<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“That they would drink from the Mortal Cup. That they would, like the first of the warrior race, Jonathan Shadowhunter, sip the blood of an angel. That they would, if they were lucky, be transformed on the spot into real, full-blooded Shadowhunters.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The character death in this was just so… pointless. It completely ruined the story for me and ruined all the previous happiness that happened on Magnus’ couch. This is the final story in the anthology, and it concludes Simon’s two-year journey of being in the academy. All the enjoyment that I had from the start of this one just really just fell flat by that ending. And I think it really left the entire collection off on a bad and sour note, if I’m being completely honest. I don’t even know how I feel about him honoring the last name. Yikes.<br><br>I gave <i>Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy</i> three stars overall, because out of a possible 50 stars (5 stars possible for each of the 10 stories) this collection accumulated 36 stars <b>(72%)</b>! <br><br><a href="https://meltotheany.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/meltotheany/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://meltotheany.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC4RbHEg_fH6CewJrh_0xJ9g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="http://www.twitch.tv/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitch</a> <br><br>Buddy read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/68490752-kaya" rel="nofollow noopener">Kaya</a> at <a href="https://afictionalbookworm.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">A Fictional Bookworm</a>! ❤</span>
  <a data-text-id="9967077495417216670" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

BOOK. <br/><br/>Now, I read Lady Midnight before this, not know it would spoil me a bit, but I still loved reading and learning about some of the backstory to the things I read about in LM! <br/><br/>I was so happy to be with Simon again because Simon was easily one of my top three favs in The Mortal Instruments...hell, even in the entirety of The Shadowhunter Chronicles he's my favorite! <br/><br/>What I also enjoyed about this bindup was how many flashbacks there were!   <span id="freeText7410939521691907497" style="display:none">I absolutely LOVED. THIS. BOOK. <br /><br />Now, I read Lady Midnight before this, not know it would spoil me a bit, but I still loved reading and learning about some of the backstory to the things I read about in LM! <br /><br />I was so happy to be with Simon again because Simon was easily one of my top three favs in The Mortal Instruments...hell, even in the entirety of The Shadowhunter Chronicles he's my favorite! <br /><br />What I also enjoyed about this bindup was how many flashbacks there were! We visited Will &amp; Tessa, James Herondale, Robert Lightwood in the days of the Circle, and so many others! I really really loved reading about these past events and getting a look at a different perspective. <br /><br />And I even loved the new characters we were introduced to just as much! Marisol was easily one of my favorites along with George (which is probably a given with a lot of others.) I loved the humor and the sarcasm and everything about this book and this bindup and these stories. EVERYTHING. </span>

<div id="review_1421514099" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="mith" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7621359-mith"><img alt="mith" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586053966p2/7621359.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1421514099?book_show_action=true">Oct 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="mith" class="user" itemprop="url" name="mith" href="/user/show/7621359-mith">mith</a>
      </span>

          marked it as maybe-read




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7621359-mith?shelf=2016-publication">2016-publication</a>
          </div>

  <span id="freeText2626033983943940703" style="display:none">Hey guuuuys! Look, the actual cover is out now!<br><br>(I mean I doubt I'll read this bc I'm not a big fan of novellas or bind-ups in general, but y'know, one day.)<br>Since I was bored and detest calculus homework, I decided to put all the covers of the novellas together.<br>So, uh, here:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445395328i/16643560.png" width="400" height="241" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>and because I have no doubt that's tiny as hell: hopefully, <a href="https://36.media.tumblr.com/337895723c70a57ca672cf68f278b83c/tumblr_nwju4rYN7J1r4w9bno1_1280.png" rel="nofollow noopener">this'll be a higher def.</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="2626033983943940703" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1903331585" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1903331585" />
    <a title="Althea | themoonwholistens ☾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/59033840-althea-themoonwholistens"><img alt="Althea | themoonwholistens ☾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597139554p2/59033840.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1903331585?book_show_action=true">Nov 06, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Althea | themoonwholistens ☾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Althea | themoonwholistens ☾" href="/user/show/59033840-althea-themoonwholistens">Althea | themoonwholistens ☾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781406362848" href="/book/show/32718466-tales-from-the-shadowhunter-academy">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">all shadowhunter fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59033840-althea-themoonwholistens?shelf=genre-urban-fantasy">genre-urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59033840-althea-themoonwholistens?shelf=rep-lgbtq">rep-lgbtq</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59033840-althea-themoonwholistens?shelf=favourites-of-all-time">favourites-of-all-time</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1903331585" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10597916950691321822"><blockquote>
  <i>“It didn’t feel like bravery. It simply felt like taking the next step forward.”</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>I’m going to bury myself in a hole so that I can scream and cry in peace with my emotions to be whisked away by Lovelace ghosts.</b> <br/><br/>A moment of silence because these stories were so nostalgic but also creative and highly emotional. I feel like all of these short stories were essential in understand the “whys” of the conflicts and just amazing additional content for any shadowhunter fan. In case you are wondering:<br/><br/><b>I r</b></span>
  <span id="freeText10597916950691321822" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>“It didn’t feel like bravery. It simply felt like taking the next step forward.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>I’m going to bury myself in a hole so that I can scream and cry in peace with my emotions to be whisked away by Lovelace ghosts.</b> <br><br>A moment of silence because these stories were so nostalgic but also creative and highly emotional. I feel like all of these short stories were essential in understand the “whys” of the conflicts and just amazing additional content for any shadowhunter fan. In case you are wondering:<br><br><b>I recommend reading this short story collection after you’ve read The Mortal Instruments and The Infernal Devices but before The Dark Artifices and The Last Hours. </b><br><br>also I’m just simply shadowhunter trash.<br><br>The stories are so well done in this compilation and the way it kept tying back to the academy was creative. I was crying in every timeline and it gives me joy at how much content this world has. It might be intimidating from the outside but when you're in it... you're in.<br><br>everyone constantly points out the aspects of the characters that they don’t like and they find annoying but even though I respect their opinions… I just do not see it 😹 Me reading this and being once again acquainted to the TMI characters after 4 years just supports that. I don’t think there’s a character in this series that I find annoying or hate (yes I’m talking about Jace), I just really am so blinded by love.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1605084813ra/30362636.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“As long as you can find people who spoke the language of your soul, you will never be alone.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><u>Welcome to the Shadowhunter Academy:</u> ★★★★★(4.5)<br>I feel like it's the nostalgia talking but also the character relationships and dynamics built here was so cute &lt;3<br><br><u>The Lost Herondale:</u> ★★★★☆(4.0)<br>This was hearbreaking and full of foreshadowing<br><br><u>The Whitechapel Fiend:</u> ★★★★★ (4.5)<br>James is so adorableee. I want to cry. Love that this goes through a lot of the character dynamics &lt;3<br><blockquote>
  <i>“Danger is appealing, especially to those who have nothing to lose.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><u>Nothing but Shadows:</u> ★★★★★ (5.0)<br>PARABATAIS!!! WE LOVE TO SEE IT! Yeah I am actually crying. I am tempted to just skip TDA and go straight to TLH. Emotional as always. James and Matthew have my heart.<br><blockquote>
  <i>“If you saw humanity as I can see it, there is very little brightness and warmth for me... You are who you have always been. And that is enough. That is more than enough.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><u>The Evil We Love:</u> ★★★★☆ (3.5)<br>It was so interesting to see this side of the Circle and getting into the mind of Robert Lightwood and Valentine. A lot of these stories are centered around the parabatai bonds and I just love that.<br><br><u>Pale Kings and Princes:</u> ★★★☆☆ (3.5)<br>That last part though... my emotion<br><br><u>Bitter of Tongue:</u> ★★★★☆ (3.5)<br>MARK BLACKTHORN &lt;333 all of the blackthorns to be honest<br><blockquote>
  <i>“We have to be what kind of shadowhunters we wanted to be and show them.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><u>The Fiery Trial:</u> ★★★☆☆ (3.5)<br>Oh that was FUN! It was nice seeing how the parabatai ceremony works and these short stories really do add a lot to the plot and the build up.<br><br><u>Born to Endless Night:</u> ★★★★★ (4.5)<br>The highlight of this story is Robert Lightwood suggesting that Alec and Magnus <i>magicked</i> a baby. I also realized that Alec basically inherited Will’s features. Magnus Bane as a constant in every shadowhunter novel is one of the best decisions CC has made.<br><br><u>Angels Twice Descending:</u> ★★★★★ (4.5)<br>OHMYGOD JESSAMINE. I sobbed<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“The point was you lived.”</i>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="10597916950691321822" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1547694662" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1547694662" />
    <a title="Anastasia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/29194167-anastasia"><img alt="Anastasia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459611514p2/29194167.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1547694662?book_show_action=true">Feb 13, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anastasia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anastasia" href="/user/show/29194167-anastasia">Anastasia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1547694662" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5678458345998007395"><i> <b> 5/5 stars </b> </i><br/><br/>Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy is a collection of ten novellas that follows Simon Lewis after the events of City of Heavenly Fire, the last book in the Mortal Instruments series. <br/><br/><b> <i> Disclaimer: If you haven’t read the Mortal Instruments and the Infernal Devices series there will be spoilers and references ahead. </i> </b><br/><br/><i> Simon Lewis has been a human and a vampire, and now he is becoming a Shadowhunter. The events of City of Heavenly Fire left him stripped of his memories, and Simon isn</i></span>
  <span id="freeText5678458345998007395" style="display:none"><i> <b> 5/5 stars </b> </i><br /><br />Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy is a collection of ten novellas that follows Simon Lewis after the events of City of Heavenly Fire, the last book in the Mortal Instruments series. <br /><br /><b> <i> Disclaimer: If you haven’t read the Mortal Instruments and the Infernal Devices series there will be spoilers and references ahead. </i> </b><br /><br /><i> Simon Lewis has been a human and a vampire, and now he is becoming a Shadowhunter. The events of City of Heavenly Fire left him stripped of his memories, and Simon isn’t sure who he is anymore. So when the Shadowhunter Academy reopens, Simon throws himself into this new world of demon-hunting, determined to find himself again. Whomever this new Simon might be.<br /><br />But the Academy is a Shadowhunter institution, which means it has some problems. Like the fact that non-Shadowhunter students have to live in the basement. At least Simon’s trained in weaponry—even if it’s only from hours of playing D&amp;D.<br /><br />Join Simon on his journey to become a Shadowhunter, and learn about the Academy’s illustrious history along the way, through guest lecturers such as Jace Herondale, Tessa Gray, and Magnus Bane. Written by Cassandra Clare, Sarah Rees Brennan, Maureen Johnson, and Robin Wasserman, these moving and hilarious short stories are perfect for the fan who just can’t get enough of the Shadowhunters. </i> <br /><br />If you have not finished all of the novellas and you would like to read my opinion on each novella separately the links are below. Each short summary of my thoughts on the separate novellas are a quick write up I wrote immediately after reading each one. Thus, my thoughts aren’t permanent and all over the place. Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy book and review links:<br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22428828.Welcome_to_Shadowhunter_Academy__Tales_from_the_Shadowhunter_Academy___1_" rel="nofollow noopener">The Lost Herondale</a>:<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23381005.The_Evil_We_Love__Tales_from_the_Shadowhunter_Academy___5_" title="The Evil We Love (Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy, #5) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">The Evil We Love</a>:<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1579770021?book_show_action=false">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23381006.Pale_Kings_and_Princes__Tales_from_the_Shadowhunter_Academy___6_" title="Pale Kings and Princes (Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy, #6) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Pale Kings and Princes</a>:<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1579775824?book_show_action=false">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23381007.Bitter_of_Tongue__Tales_from_the_Shadowhunter_Academy___7_" title="Bitter of Tongue (Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy, #7) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Bitter of Tongue</a>:<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1584188224?book_show_action=false">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23381009.The_Fiery_Trial__Tales_from_the_Shadowhunter_Academy___8_" title="The Fiery Trial (Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy, #8) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">The Fiery Trial</a>:<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1584208790?book_show_action=false">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23381012.Born_to_Endless_Night__Tales_from_the_Shadowhunter_Academy___9_" title="Born to Endless Night (Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy, #9) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Born to Endless Night</a>:<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1586314488?book_show_action=false">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23381014.Angels_Twice_Descending__Tales_from_the_Shadowhunter_Academy___10_" title="Angels Twice Descending (Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy, #10) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Angels Twice Descending</a>:<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1587380675?book_show_action=false">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a> <br /><br /><br /><blockquote> <b> <i> “Welcome to Shadowhunter Academy,” said Catarina Loss, her voice gentle.” </i> </b> </blockquote> If Catarina Loss said this to me I would <s> probably </s> burst into flames right then and there. I have been waiting to read these because I wanted to read Lady Midnight immediately after. And boy was that a good choice. After finished all ten of the novellas I was having serious Cassandra Clare withdrawals. All I wanted was more Simon Lewis but I would definitely settle for Emma Carstairs. I absolutely loved all of the novellas, even if some of them had a few bumps in the foundation. <blockquote> <i> <b> “Speaking of people being foxy, do you mean? I’m George Lovelace,” said George. “I say my surname without shame, because I am secure in my masculinity like that.” </b> </i> </blockquote> Our <i> new </i> cast of characters is beautiful. First, we have the, mundane George Lovelace who has completely erased the prior Lovelace legacy in my eyes. He has a gorgeous, sculpted by Angel Raziel himself, body and a sexy as hell scottish drawl. In the first novella I thought he was going to be the <i> new Jace </i> but I was dead wrong. George Lovelace is the kind of guy that you would bring home to your parents. They might be apprehensive at first but when he opens their mouth your parents will be putty in his hands. George has the kind of attitude that complements Simon’s perfectly. He is kind, a little geeky now that Simon has gotten into his mind, and basically the sweetest characters you have ever met. The second mundane we meet is Marisol Garza. She is the youngest of the cast since she is only 15 and oh my goodness she is such a spitfire. She keeps up with the best in her class, including the shadowhunters, and follows the <i> say sorry later instead of ask for permission now </i>, way of life. <br /><br />Now for the shadowhunters by blood. The first student, and my favorite out of the shadowhunters, is Beatriz Mendoza, an amazing girl who doesn’t follow the stream of elitists and makes her own path instead. When Simon Lewis speaks up about showing downworlders and dregs respect she is right there beside him. She does remain friends with her fellow students Jon Cartwright and Julie Beauvale, even though their views are very different compare to those. Julie’s mother had been one of the first to be turned into an Endarkened soldier by Sebastian Morgenstern. This fact has noticeably changed her demeanor. She keeps very close to those that she knows will keep her safe and will keep her on top, such as Jon Cartwright. Jon Cartwright is a boastful and extremely rude person. He makes snide remarks about the mundane students, calling them dregs, and always talks down upon Downworlders, even his own teacher Catarina Loss. There is really nothing good to say about Jon Cartwright, except for the last 3 or so novellas when he is <i> befriended </i> by a very good influence.<br /><br />The co-writing of these novellas were very interesting. Each writing pair had their own writing style and way of portraying Simon Lewis. First there was Sarah Rees Brennan. I thought the way she described the world and situations from Simon’s point of view was a little too stiff and you could definitely tell the difference between Cassandra Clare’s portions are hers. Clare would have quick witted or sassy dialogue and descriptions but then there were stiff and very detailed descriptions with words I would never see Simon using. Maureen Johnson’s and Robin Wasserman’s writing styles on the other hand flowed very nicely with Cassandra Clares. They truly portrayed the nerdy and loveable character that we know and love, each with their own subtle twist. <blockquote> <i> <b> “You love, and tremble, and burn. Do not let any of them tell you who you are. You are the flame that cannot be put out. You are the star that cannot be lost. You are who you have always been, and that is enough and more than enough. Anyone who looks at you and sees darkness is blind.” </b> </i> </blockquote> My favorite parts of each novella were the flashbacks. We were given stories about William Herondale, personally my favorite, Jem Carstairs, Tessa Gray, Robert Lightwood, the Circle, and many others. Each one giving me intense chest pains because of how beautiful they were. If you aren’t fully committed to reading a 600+ page collection of novellas about Simon Lewis do it for the flashbacks. <br /><br />All in all Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy was an amazing collection of novellas. The novellas take place over the span of two years and each one covered a substantial amount of time. None of them felt rushed or spaced out too much. Cassandra Clare, Sarah Rees Brennan, Maureen Johnson, and Robin Wasserman did a great job writing them and I will definitely be reading The Bane Chronicles now that I know I enjoy the short story bind ups. Each novella gave us new details and characters that I hope will be applied to Lady Midnight because that would make the story ten times better. I recommend this bind up for everyone who has finished the Mortal Instruments and the Infernal Devices. <i> The Infernal Devices isn’t necessary but it does help with some of the flashbacks. </i> </span>
  <a data-text-id="5678458345998007395" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1848244114" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1848244114" />
    <a title="Jiana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10502567-jiana"><img alt="Jiana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1540380229p2/10502567.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1848244114?book_show_action=true">Mar 20, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jiana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jiana" href="/user/show/10502567-jiana">Jiana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1848244114" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3833218597591763074">Buddy read with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/57334157-caitlin' rel='nofollow noopener'>Cait</a>!<br/><br/>I'm not going to go into details with each novella because there's a gazillion of them and I've already some forgotten details here and there.<br/><br/><u>Rating for each novella:</u><br/>1) <b>Welcome to the Shadowhunter Academy</b>: 3 stars<br/>2) <b>The Lost Herondale</b>: 3.5 stars<br/>3) <b>The Whitechapel Fiend</b>: 4 stars<br/>4) <b>Nothing but Shadows</b>: 5 stars<br/>5) <b>The Evil We Love</b>: 3.5 stars<br/>6) <b>Pale Kings and Princes</b>: 4.5 stars<br/>7) <b>Bitter of Tongue</b>: 5 stars<br/>8) <b>The Fiery Trial</b>: 2.5 stars<br/>9) <b>Born to Endless Night</b>: 4 stars<br/>10) <b>Angels Twi</b></span>
  <span id="freeText3833218597591763074" style="display:none">Buddy read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/57334157-caitlin" rel="nofollow noopener">Cait</a>!<br /><br />I'm not going to go into details with each novella because there's a gazillion of them and I've already some forgotten details here and there.<br /><br /><u>Rating for each novella:</u><br />1) <b>Welcome to the Shadowhunter Academy</b>: 3 stars<br />2) <b>The Lost Herondale</b>: 3.5 stars<br />3) <b>The Whitechapel Fiend</b>: 4 stars<br />4) <b>Nothing but Shadows</b>: 5 stars<br />5) <b>The Evil We Love</b>: 3.5 stars<br />6) <b>Pale Kings and Princes</b>: 4.5 stars<br />7) <b>Bitter of Tongue</b>: 5 stars<br />8) <b>The Fiery Trial</b>: 2.5 stars<br />9) <b>Born to Endless Night</b>: 4 stars<br />10) <b>Angels Twice Descending</b>: 3 stars<br /><br /><i>
  <blockquote>“You are the flame that cannot be put out. You are the star that cannot be lost. You are who you have always been, and that is enough and more than enough. Anyone who looks at you and sees the darkness is blind.”</blockquote>
</i><br /><br />I'm always excited to read anything related to Shadowhunter universe. I adore this world, I adore the characters and I always <b>want</b> more. Now, there's quite a mix in my individual ratings: some novellas were super boring or pointless or I honestly could've been just fine if I hadn't read them and some were great. However, overall, it was good collection! What I liked about these novellas was that they weren't all about Simon's experience in the Academy. Some were focused on characters we know from TMI, TID, and TDA. We see:<br />- Will, Jem, and Tessa and the next generation, i.e. the kids in both The Whitechapel Fiend and Nothing but Shadows<br />- Julian Blackthorn and Emma Carstairs and the Blackthorn family in The Fiery Trial and Bitter of Tongue<br />- Helen Blackthorn in Pale Kings and Princes<br />- Mark Blackthorn (<b>a.k.a my everything</b>) in Bitter of Tongue; obviously I gave that 5 stars just for him. <br />- Magnus and Alec in Born to Endless Night<br />- Isabelle, Clary and Jace in several of these novellas, especially Isabelle since she obviously has a big role in Simon's life. <br />- Finally, The Evil We Love is focused on Robert Lightwood and his younger days with Valentine and the circle.<br /><br />The two novellas relating to TID and the next generation? Those were <u>brilliant</u>. I absolutely <i>can't wait</i> for Chain of Thorns (Book 1 - The Last Hours trilogy) because I'm already so in love with these characters! The wait is now painful.<br /><br />Some novellas provided a base for Lady Midnight. While it's recommended to read this before Lady Midnight, it won't matter at all if you read Lady Midnight first, as I did. Everything is explained either way. <br /><br />Of course, my favorite novella would be Bitter of Tongue. Why? Mark Blackthorn, of course! I absolutely <b>adore</b> him and I missed him so much, so seeing him again made me smile like an idiot. <br /><br />My least favorite novella would have to be The Fiery Trial. I found it to be very confusing and utterly pointless, to be honest. What the novella revealed wasn't at all shocking. If anything, I'm pretty sure every single person who's read TMI and knows about the general plot of this book/novella bind-up (even if they haven't read it yet), already know this "reveal" was going to happen. So, yeah. Nah.<br /><br /><i>
  <blockquote>“I think sometimes it's too hard to believe in yourself. You just do the things you're not sure you can do. You just act, in spite of not being certain. I don't believe I can change the world--it sounds stupid to even talk about it--but I'm going to try.”</blockquote>
</i><br /><br />I didn't particularly care for any of the new characters introduced except George Lovelace. George is precious. George is adorable. George is an angel. <br /><br />In addition to that, these novellas also centered around Simon and Isabelle's relationship. So much drama went on, which is 100% understandable. I am absolute trash for this ship and when they finally got together again, I was beyond happy.<br /><br />Now. The final novella. It would've been a great novella if it weren't for that ending. I basically spoiled myself about the ending and I got pissed at it. I dreaded reaching it and I'm still pissed now. IT WAS SO UNCALLED FOR AND UNNECESSARY. I don't get why it happened?? What was the point??? WHY, WHY, WHY? Things would've been totally fine if it hadn't happened. I'm not happy, okay. Not. happy. at. all. I refuse this ending. This is all.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3833218597591763074" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1767985532" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1767985532" />
    <a title="Caitlin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/57334157-caitlin"><img alt="Caitlin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1507948675p2/57334157.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1767985532?book_show_action=true">Mar 20, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Caitlin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Caitlin" href="/user/show/57334157-caitlin">Caitlin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781406362848" href="/book/show/32718466-tales-from-the-shadowhunter-academy">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57334157-caitlin?shelf=novellas">novellas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57334157-caitlin?shelf=3-stars">3-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57334157-caitlin?shelf=2017-read">2017-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1767985532" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12029114009306610289">Buddy read with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1848244114?book_show_action=false&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jia!</a><br/><br/>Okay, I liked this book for the most part but there were definitely sections that dragged on that I gave 0 shits about. I think in the end I ended up actually really liking 3 of these novellas, while the other 7 I didn't overly care for. Basically my main problem was the fact that Simon is my least favourite character from TMI. I find him annoying as all hell and I really struggled to get past that. As you'll see, my favourite novellas were ones that he had very limited role </span>
  <span id="freeText12029114009306610289" style="display:none">Buddy read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1848244114?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Jia!</a><br /><br />Okay, I liked this book for the most part but there were definitely sections that dragged on that I gave 0 shits about. I think in the end I ended up actually really liking 3 of these novellas, while the other 7 I didn't overly care for. Basically my main problem was the fact that Simon is my least favourite character from TMI. I find him annoying as all hell and I really struggled to get past that. As you'll see, my favourite novellas were ones that he had very limited role in. I just feel like he's a useless character and I would 10/10 sacrifice him (sorry Amber).<br /><br /><b>Welcome to the Shadowhunter Academy</b> - 2.5 stars<br /><br /><i>"We all want to be heroes, but you know you can be one. You know in another life, in an alternate universe, however you want to think of it, you were a hero. You can one again."</i><br /><br />Basically this novella was just introducing Simon and us as readers to the Shadowhunter Academy which is basically a dump now. We meet a whole bunch of new characters that we will be seeing throughout the novellas - mainly George Lovelace, who is Simon's roommate. We also get more in depth into Izzy and Simon's (lack of a) relationship now that Simon has no memory of them being together basically. Look, this drama pissed me off throughout the entire book. <br /><br /><b>The Lost Herondale</b> - 2.5 stars<br /><br />Look, I've got nothing to say about this novella. There's a missing Herondale child somewhere in the world and since I've read <i>Lady Midnight</i>, I know who that is. Amazing. The end. <br /><br /><b>The Whitechapel Fiend</b> - 4 stars<br /><br /><i>"I am Tessa Gray and I believe in the importance of stories."</i><br /><br />Tessa comes into the Shadowhunter Academy to share some stories and she tells the story of how she actually knows the true identity of Jack the Ripper since they had to deal with those issues back in the day. Look, this was one of the best novellas since a) Tessa and Will are amazing and I love them and b) it's about Jack the Ripper which is always a great story to hear about since I loved reading <i>Stalking Jack the Ripper</i> a little while ago. <b>The best part of this entire novella (and the book in general) was Will and Tessa's son, James, running around yelling "SPOON" at everyone while he held a spoon.</b><br /><br /><b>Nothing but Shadows</b> - 4 stars<br /><br /><i>"You are the flame that cannot be put out. You are the star that cannot be lost. You are who you have always been, and that is enough and more than enough. Anyone who looks at you and sees the darkness is blind."</i><br /><br />In this novella we follow James Herondale (the spoon boy) who's now 13 and is now attending the Shadowhunter Academy. It basically tells the story of how Matthew and James went from enemies to <i>parabatai</i>. We also learn a little bit more about James' gifts and how Tessa being a warlock has influenced who he is today.<br /><br /><b>The Evil We Love</b> - 3 stars<br /><br /><i>"He would accept Valentine's offer. He would let Valentine choose for him, let Valentine believe for him. He would do whatever he needed to hang on to Valentine, and to the circle and to it's cause. It was all he had left."</i><br /><br />We follow Robert Lightwood in reliving the beginnings of the Circle which was run by Valentine and basically started all the shit that happened in TMI. Robert was <i>parabatai</i> to Micahel Wayland and they were best friends until Michael confessed that he was in love with Robert, which basically resulted in Robert being extremely loyal to Valentine and losing his way. It also kinda explains why he would be semi-homophobic when Alec came out all those years later.<br /><br /><b>Pale Kings and Princes</b> - 3 stars<br /><br /><i>"Trust a faerie at your own risk, because they are for nothing but themselves. They sow nothing but destruction. And their preferred weapon is human love."</i><br /><br />Basically Simon and Izzy's relationship really started to go to shit and it really got on my nerves in this one. Also we had Helen Blackthorn come and tell the students about how she came to be basically and that her dad and uncle were captured by the Fair Folk - thus resulting in both Helen and Mark Blackthorn. I mean, I've heard this story in <i>Lady Midnight</i>, so I was pretty bored in it. <br /><br /><b>Bitter of Tongue</b> - 3 stars<br /><br /><i>"You are Mark of the Wild Hunt. You ride on the air, a hundred dizzy wheeling miles above them all. They will never hurt you again, save that you let them. Do not let them."</i><br /><br />Simon somehow gets captured by the Fair Folk, where he meets Mark Blackthorn. It was actually interesting to see Mark where he wasn't completely fucked up by the Wild Hunt. Basically he still thinks the Shadowhunters are going to come and save him - but they're definitely not. It really explains why he acted the way he did in <i>Lady Midnight</i>. <br /><br /><b>The Fiery Trial</b> - 2 stars<br /><br /><i>"It makes sense. You and me. I feel like it's always been true. It's always what we were."</i><br /><br />What the fuck was this novella. I was confused for the entirety of it and when it was explained why it all happened, I eye rolled so hard. What a shocker, Clary and Simon are "true <i>parabatai</i>". Amazing. Never saw that coming. I just eye rolled so hard again thinking about how lame this one was. We also get to see Julian and Emma become <i>parabatai</i> which was good to see them and the gang again. I think this was my least favourite of the novellas tbh. <br /><br /><b>Born to Endless Night</b> - 4 stars<br /><br /><i>"He had thought he lived life believing a thousand possibilities were open to him. But he had not thought of this possibility as being open to him: family life like mundanes and Nephilim had, love so secure that it could be shared with someone bran-new to the world and helpless."</i><br /><br />This was my favourite novella because Simon and Izzy finally fixed their shitty drama. Also, the best part was obviously Malec moments. A blue baby warlock was randomly found at the Academy and Magnus and Alec decided to adopt him and name him Max (after Alec and Izzy's brother). It was honestly so sweet and adorable and this was the one I've been really looking forward to reading for ages!<br /><br /><b>Angels Twice Descending</b> - 3.5 stars<br /><br /><i>"and his veins burn with angel fire and he is the Simon he once was and the Simon he then became and the Simon he now will be, he endures and he is reborn, he is blood and flesh and spark of the divine. He is Nephilim."</i><br /><br />Okay, so I already knew how this book was going to end (thanks Jia for the spoiler). I'm actually pretty annoyed that that certain event happened. Like, it was so unnecessary and not at all needed. The only character I god damn liked and now this happens to them. Rude. This is an attack and I would like to know why the hell that needed to happen. Everything could have been fine. But nope. Screw you all. <br /><br />Okay honestly the more I think about this ending the madder I get. It was pointless. It honestly feels to me that Cassie didn't know how to tie up this one loose end so she took drastic measures to quickly solve the problem. It wasn't needed at all and I'm actually really annoyed by this.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12029114009306610289" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14248273381229410141">5/5 ☆ i'm a mess of emotions. <br/><br/>i didn't realize but there are a ton of (i guess you could say) side characters i didn't fully appreciate or understand until reading these novellas and i'm so happy my perspective changed. it shows there are more sides to a person you may think.<br/><br/>i'm also surprised by how strongly i appreciated the themes. these novellas are mostly about finding who you are and what YOU want. i fohnd that really surprising because most novella collections are just compilations of "fa</span>
  <span id="freeText14248273381229410141" style="display:none">5/5 ☆ i'm a mess of emotions. <br /><br />i didn't realize but there are a ton of (i guess you could say) side characters i didn't fully appreciate or understand until reading these novellas and i'm so happy my perspective changed. it shows there are more sides to a person you may think.<br /><br />i'm also surprised by how strongly i appreciated the themes. these novellas are mostly about finding who you are and what YOU want. i fohnd that really surprising because most novella collections are just compilations of "fan-fiction-esque" writings and lack depth. all these stories had a moral and made me love the shadowhunter world even more than i already do. <br /><br />another thing i loved about this collection was that it didn't feeeeeeel long (which, it is quite long) or disconnected. i usually have a hard time getting into novellas because they're so short and don't connect together into one cohesive story, but TALES FROM THE SHADOWHUNTER ACADEMY was not the case. it felt like one whole book split into 12 parts instead of 12 parts put together as a book.<br /><br />///FULL REVIEW + DISCUSSION (maybe) TO COME///</span>

<div id="review_1449307002" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Sharon" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23218431-sharon"><img alt="Sharon" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1563502369p2/23218431.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1449307002?book_show_action=true">Jan 02, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1449307002" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13971020196898411249">Here are some of my thoughts:<br/>•	I adore the one about James Herondale and Matthew Fairchild. It is so sweet and funny – ahhhh. <br/>•	Fuck you, Robert Lightwood, always, but I can finally understand his perspective a bit more – while still being disgusted by his guts, but also, still appreciating that he’s trying to change for his children. <br/>•	Helen’s story breaks my heart (and the real fae story is shocking but somewhat eye-opening). <br/>•	Jem is always a light in the dark. Seeing how he has been there fo</span>
  <span id="freeText13971020196898411249" style="display:none">Here are some of my thoughts:<br />•	I adore the one about James Herondale and Matthew Fairchild. It is so sweet and funny – ahhhh. <br />•	Fuck you, Robert Lightwood, always, but I can finally understand his perspective a bit more – while still being disgusted by his guts, but also, still appreciating that he’s trying to change for his children. <br />•	Helen’s story breaks my heart (and the real fae story is shocking but somewhat eye-opening). <br />•	Jem is always a light in the dark. Seeing how he has been there for Will, Tessa, and James in every way. <br />•	AGH Will – I smile-cry with how he keeps on making up excuses to visit Jem.<br />•	Mark Blackthorn breaks my heart. I’m glad that he gets to send that sweet message via Simon to Helen on her wedding though.<br />•	The Malec chapter – it is so cute with the baby. I like seeing Magnus interacting with Catarina and reminiscing about Ragnor Fell and Raphael – really makes me feel for them. Furthermore, I can see Magnus and Alec’s relationship getting stronger and they’re adorable awwww. I’m glad to see Alec having a purpose in his life and gaining a quiet confidence as well. Also, it is funny to see the older Lightwoods being all gushy and controlling and actually nice? I love the Lightwood family LOL. Very nice chapter. <br />•	Overall, I can definitely see Clare setting up her spinoffs with the side characters we see here. It has been fun to read about Simon and about characters we know about AND characters that we didn’t know much about before.<br />•	I like the new characters. George is such a cinnamonroll – he is the sweetest, nicest guy and HILARIOUS. Marisol is badass and I love how she has gotten Jon to warm up to her and want to hear her “mundane” facts. His character development is on point. Julie and Beatriz have also changed for the better along with Jon. I like them all as a friends group. <br />•	Sizzy is my OTP and this book had me on pins and needles waiting for them to be all right and good and happy and together. THEY ARE SO CUTE AGH. I love them more than ever before. They are just so cute, perfect, vulnerable, and honest.<br />•	It is great to see Simon learning and growing in this book. He tries to reconcile Simon-before-memory-loss and Simon-after-memory-loss-with-distorted-mundane-memories, but thankfully we still have geeky, lovable Simon. However, because he is conflicted with these two sides, he does learn to be an even newer Simon – a Simon who is aware of his two different pasts and wants to find himself through the Shadowhunter Academy. He definitely has learned many lessons about himself and about the world. He has accepted all sides of himself, and is moving forward to a future he has chosen – I love how we see this progression in him. I am glad to see him actually seeking changes to bring equality and fairness to the shadowhunters. He sees the problems, and I love how he is passionate and determined to continue changing what he can. I hope he gets the Conclave to reform because damn, they’re pretty terrible at times.<br />•	I simultaneously love and hate the side stories interwoven into Simon’s main storyline. I love it because they’re interesting and informative. I hate it because damn I really want to hear what’s going on with Simon the most.<br /><br />I think I have forgotten my earnest love for TMI books. I mean…not that I have started disliking them or anything, but it has been a few years since I have read one, and I have been so skeptical to read the new stuff because this series has a way of having my mind mesmerized by these characters’ lives, and I was scared that the books would dim the good memories I already have of this series. Anyway, this series has easily gotten my mind back in the shadowhunter world’s mindset and it is so easy to love these characters who are so fleshed-out and unique. I have enjoyed these tales of Simon (mostly Simon but honestly about a lot of other characters as well), and I honestly would like to hear more about his adventures. <b>4 stars</b><br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[What the fuckkkkk???? This wasn’t supposed to make me cry. Only a few pages towards the end, and I was feeling safe and good and happy, and BAM – Clare had to do something to rip my heart out. WHY OH WHY. Specifically: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[GEORGE WHYYYYYYY. He was the one new character that shouldn’t have died. I CAN’T DEAL. FUCK FUCK FUCK FUCK. I mean I’m glad we got to see the ghost of him at the end (twice, so I’m assuming it was real), and the Lovelace (Jessamine, is that you???) took him in. But mannnn I love him so much. Clare has to write an afterlife story for him because this feels so unfair. I’m literally not over it. I feel like this is the one thing that shouldn’t have been in this book because it’s just toooo much sadness. Ahhh. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br /><u>Things that you might want to know <b>(WARNING: Spoilers below)</b></u><br />Happy/satisfying ending? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Bittersweet. Mainly happy, except for one very sad event that I already named in the spoiler above. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />Love triangle? Cheating? Angst level? Other things to note? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No, no, switches back from low-medium-high. Some chapters are chill. Some chapters filled me with angst. <br /><br />Simon is completely dedicated to Isabelle. Two girls had a crush on him, but he felt nothing because he was utterly focused on Isabelle. Isabelle was presumably faithful to him as well (they were not talking for a few months because he shunned her in the beginning, so we don’t know what she was doing on her own. Moping? Definitely. Nothing else was said. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />Tears-worthy? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Fuck yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />Humor? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yesss. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />Favorite scenes? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Sizzy scenes always &lt;3 Like their first REAL date that we saw. Them at the Lightwood party at Malec’s place. When Isabelle and Simon talked about loving each other no matter what (no matter if he chose to be mundane or not). Malec scenes, like when they were talking about taking care of the baby together and getting married some day. Marisol and Jon being funny and cute. George and Simon hanging out and George making funny comments, and George telling Simon he’s his best friend – aw. The Lightwood taking care of the baby – everyone doing something, and Jace and Clary are just chilling.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />What age level would be appropriate? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Teens and up. Vague mentions of sex. Vague mentions of torture. No gory details.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /></span>

Ghosts of the Shadow Market ★★★★<br /><br />-----------------------------------------------<br /><br /><b>Welcome to the Shadowhunter Academy</b><br />★★★★<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Everybody in this academy, Shadowhunters and mundanes, people with the Sight and without it, every one of them is looking to be a hero. We are all hoping for it, and trying for it, and soon we will be bleeding for it. You’re just like the rest of us, Si. Except there’s one thing about you that’s different: We all want to be heroes, but you know you can be one. You know in another life, in an alternate universe, however you want to think of it, you were a hero. You can be one again. Maybe not the same hero, but you have it in you to make the right choices, to make the big sacrifices. That’s a lot of pressure. But it’s a lot more hope than any of the rest of us have. Think about it that way, Simon Lewis, and I think you’re pretty lucky.”</i>
</b><br /><br />2016 - OH SIMON HOW I'VE MISSED YOU! Also, I LOVE George!<br /><br />2020 - Knowing how these stories end, reading this is so depressing omg. The friendship between Simon and George is EVERYTHING.<br /><br /><b>The Lost Herondale</b><br />★★★<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“We are all what our pasts have made us,” Catarina said. “The accumulation of thousands of daily choices. We can change ourselves, but never erase what we’ve been.”</i>
</b><br /><br />2020 - this one was lowkey kinda boring lol. I think from what I can remember, this is probably my least favourite cassie clare anthology? But we shall see!<br /><br /><b>The Whitechapel Fiend</b><br />★★★★<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“To his children, Will showed the same love he had always shown to her, fierce and unyielding. And the same protectiveness he had only ever showed to one other person: the person James had been named after. Will’s parabatai, Jem.”</i>
</b><br /><br />2016 - SO MANY OF MY FAVE CHARACTERS IN THIS ONE &lt;3<br /><br />2020 - oh my gosh, baby james herondale yelling 'spoon' is the highlight of this entire book lol<br /><br /><b>Nothing But Shadows</b><br />★★★★★<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Do not let any of them tell you who you are. You are the flame that cannot be put out. You are the star that cannot be lost. You are who you have always been, and that is enough and more than enough. Anyone who looks at you and sees darkness is blind.”</i>
</b><br /><br />2016 - THIS ONE WAS AMAZING<br /><br />2020 - rereading this after reading chain of gold is EVERYTHING. I love these characters SO MUCH. <br /><br /><b>The Evil We Love</b><br />★★.5<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Love, real love, is being seen. Being known. Knowing the ugliest part of someone, and loving them anyway. And... I guess I think two people in love become something else, something more than the sum of their parts, you know? That it must be like you’re creating a new world that exists just for the two of you. You’re gods of your own pocket universe.”</i>
</b><br /><br />2020 - yooooo this was boring lol<br /><br /><b>Pale Kings and Princes</b><br />★★★<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“It's hard to believe how much light you can find in the darkness, when you have someone who loves you.”</i>
</b><br /><br />2020 - I love helen and aline with my whole heart. <br /><br /><b>Bitter of Tongue</b><br />★★★<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Every night, no matter what has happened during the day, no matter if I am torn and bloodied or so bone-tired I wish I were dead, I look up at the stars and I give each star a brother's name or a sister's face. I will not sleep until I remember every one. The stars will burn out before I forget.”</i>
</b><br /><br />2020 - this story is so bittersweet. On the one hand, seeing mark was so sad, but then aline and helen's wedding??? I love them. <br /><br /><b>The Fiery Trial</b><br />★★★.5<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“It was nice, Simon thought, in the midst of all the terrible things that could happen and sometimes did happen, there was always this. There was a lot of love.”</i>
</b><br /><br />2016 - this one was WEIRD<br /><br />2020 - this was super weird.. but I kinda enjoyed it???<br /><br /><b>Born to Endless Night</b><br />★★★★.5<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I never want anything but this, I never want a less strange love.”</i>
</b><br /><br />2016 - :')<br /><br />2020 - if I wasn't already about to have a baby, this woulda given me massive baby fever oh ma LORD<br /><br /><b>Angels Twice Descending</b><br />★★★★<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“It's not cowardly to make a choice about what you want your life to be. Choosing what's right for you, maybe that's the bravest thing you can do.”</i>
</b><br /><br />2016 - I guessed what was going to happen early on in this novella series, but it still hurt :(<br /><br />2020 - will I ever forgive cassandra clare for this? Nope, definitely not. <br /><br />Overall Rating: 3.65<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13959300875498375821" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
