<div id="review_2060820229" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2060820229" />
    <a title="✨    jamieson   ✨" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7706640-jamieson"><img alt="✨    jamieson   ✨" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499961431p2/7706640.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2060820229?book_show_action=true">Jul 20, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✨    jamieson   ✨" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✨    jamieson   ✨" href="/user/show/7706640-jamieson">✨    jamieson   ✨</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=2017-reads">2017-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=completed-series">completed-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2060820229" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8875090409655883465">I had so many mixed thoughts coming into this, because there were some elements I knew I'd like (DARK ARTIFICES CHARACTERS APPEARING, MAGNUS & ALEC!) but also some elements I really knew I wouldn't <br/><br/><b>two massive unpopular opinions I have</b><br/><br/>1: sizzy is a shit couple<br/>2: simon isn't that interesting of a character. I mean he's okay, but I don't like him that much either<br/><br/>Those elements did, kind of annoy me. But the other elements I knew I'd like I <i>really</i> liked so that kind of counter-balanced my salt. <br/><br/><i>
  </i></span>
  <span id="freeText8875090409655883465" style="display:none">I had so many mixed thoughts coming into this, because there were some elements I knew I'd like (DARK ARTIFICES CHARACTERS APPEARING, MAGNUS &amp; ALEC!) but also some elements I really knew I wouldn't <br><br><b>two massive unpopular opinions I have</b><br><br>1: sizzy is a shit couple<br>2: simon isn't that interesting of a character. I mean he's okay, but I don't like him that much either<br><br>Those elements did, kind of annoy me. But the other elements I knew I'd like I <i>really</i> liked so that kind of counter-balanced my salt. <br><br><i>
  <blockquote>“Why should we isolate people who are brave enough to try to become like us--who want to help people? Why should we treat them as if they're less than us, until they prove their worthiness or die? I won't do it.” </blockquote>
</i><br><br><u>1) Welcome to the Shadowhunter Academy: 3 stars</u><br><br>I thought the first story was just okay. It was introductory so I guess it's hard to make it super super exciting but I did just kind of find it boring and meandering. Nothing really happened and it dragged on and seemed a little too info-dumpy. <br><br><br><u>2) The Lost Herondale: 3 stars</u><br>This was interesting but since I've read lm/los and know what happens it was kind of underwhelming. I think it would have been more exciting if I'd read this before the dark artifices. But it was okay, I liked that Catarina got to be more prominent. <br><br><br><u>3) The Whitechapel Fiend: 3.5 stars</u><br>I <b>loved</b> that Will and Tessa appeared and all the others from The Infernal Devices. I liked the relationship between Tessa and Cecily was developed and that this was about Jack the Ripper! It was overall pretty fun and interesting but something about it felt a little ... unsatisfying?<br><br><u>4) Nothing but Shadows: 4 stars</u><br>Jamie was so interesting and this story got me so excited for The Last Hours. I loved seeing Will again, of course. I also loved the introduction of Matthew Fairchild and Christopher Lightwood. They were both really interesting and I can't wait to see more of them in Chain of Gold. Jamie being able to shape into a shadow is really wild to be honest and should be good to see that explored more too. Also Matthew and Jamie are cute parabatai<br><br><u>5) The Evil We Love: 2 stars</u><br>Probably my least favourite of the novellas. I just found it boring, and I find Valentine boring now. WE GET IT. Also, the thing with Robert and Michael was so unnecessary ? There was a lot of homophobia which wasn't really addressed and I don't know this story just didn't sit right with me I didn't like it much. <br><br><br><u>6) Pale Kings and Princes: 3 stars</u><br>The setting in Faerie, and it being about Mark and Helens parents was super appealing. The story of Andrew and Arthur was a little vague so it was nice it was set straight for me. The twist at the end had me shook. But this one also had a lot of Simon and Izzy which I obviously couldn't get into becayse I hate them lmao <br><br><br><u>7) Bitter of Tongue: 4 stars</u><br>Really liked this one since it features Mark Blackthorn. I found this story the most emotional of them all. I liked reading this AFTER I had read lm/los because it shines such a different and kind of sad light on the characters. It got me super upset about Julian Blackthorn and how dirty he got did in all honesty. BuT ALSO IT MADE ME MADE KIERAN IS SUCH A RAT I HATE HIM. <br><br><u>8) The Fiery Trial: 3.5 stars</u><br>SOBBING ON THE FLOOR. Love the Blackthorns so much love Emma love Jules love their family. I got super emo when Livvy came up might have shed a little tear. Was interesting to see them again as kids and see Jules taking on his role as parent. Also glad I read this one after Lady Midnight and Lord of Shadows because it let me see the Blackthorns in retrospect and that was nice. <br><br><u>9) Born to Endless Night: 5 stars</u><br>Easily my favourite of the novellas. I love Alec and Magnus so much and how their characters have grown both as a couple and individually. Alec is my favourite character in The Mortal Instruments and his happiness means the world to me. I can't believe he gets to raise a family with the man of his life we are so blessed. <br><br><br><u>10) Angels Twice Descending: 3 stars</u><br>I found this one kind of slow too but the ending left me super shooked and now I'm mad. I liked the description of the ascending ceremony since it's always been quite vague and it was good worlbuilding, and I liked the choices Simon made too. I am just mad about what happened at the end. Also way too much Sizzy. <br><br><br><b>A THREAD OF ME REACTING TO EACH CHARACTERS APPEARANCE</b><br>Everytime Alec came up:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455732565ra/18143654.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Everytime a character from The Infernal Devices appeared<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1500555839i/23357736.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Everytime a Blackthorn came up and I had to think about the injustice done to them<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1500555839i/23357735._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Everytime Sizzy came up:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1500555839i/23357739.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Me everytime a character said something racist<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1500555839i/23357734.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Me when everyone started disrespecting Helen Blackthorn and Magnus Bane<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1500556010i/23357764._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Me when they started talking about Raphael<br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>Me at the end<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1500555839i/23357737._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>George by the end of this<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1500555839i/23357733.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br>Anyway actual rating is 3.5 stars! I've read all of The Shadowhunter Chronicles now I feel accomplished and also pleased I can delete all the individually listed novellas from my tbr</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15335513126705769222">you guys holy shoot<br/>my favorite hecking character gets his own book and <br/>it<br/>is<br/>BEAUTIFUL. <br/><br/>so many lessons learned, so many themes explored, and so many stories told. each aspect was incredible and insightful and I love every single page. the last shattered me and yet made my heart whole again. I swear my heart has grown from it. there is SO MUCH LOVE for every single moment between these characters and each of their stories and I will forever cherish them all.</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Irene△⃒⃘➰" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Irene△⃒⃘➰" href="/user/show/55991704-irene">Irene△⃒⃘➰</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/55991704-irene?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1652115836" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5512308508356552488"><b>4.8/5</b><br/><br/><b>That’s what I really wanted to read about Simon!</b> I hoped to read the reactions he had after everything that had happened to him.<br/>I always liked him, I can relate so much to him, all his nerdiness and stuff, that’s me lol<br/><b>After the events happened in the main series I thought I’d lost him</b>. I didn’t care if he was taking this journey to become a Shadowhunter, for me he wasn’t the same as he was, no matter what.<br/>AND in this book he is feeling exactly the same, and that's why I mainly loved it. <br/>We</span>
  <span id="freeText5512308508356552488" style="display:none"><b>4.8/5</b><br /><br /><b>That’s what I really wanted to read about Simon!</b> I hoped to read the reactions he had after everything that had happened to him.<br />I always liked him, I can relate so much to him, all his nerdiness and stuff, that’s me lol<br /><b>After the events happened in the main series I thought I’d lost him</b>. I didn’t care if he was taking this journey to become a Shadowhunter, for me he wasn’t the same as he was, no matter what.<br />AND in this book he is feeling exactly the same, and that's why I mainly loved it. <br />We really see him struggling with his memories and trying to please the people who know him so well.<br />It’s thanks to this that <b>his character development is so on point</b> that in the end I ended up loving this Simon, with all his insecurities, in a completely new role, with new people and new relationships.<br />At the same time he still sees his old friends and all these dynamics between all of them are a big yes. <br /><b>I was so scared that this decision was going to “ruin” this character that I always liked throughout the entires series, but fortunately this didn’t happen</b>, because it’s just what I had in mind that I read, and I’m so glad.<br />_________<br /><br /><b>Special mention here goes to the Malec novella</b>, I was screaming during the entire story and it was hard to focus on the other ones (hey it’s the second to last one, it’s pretty hard not constantly thinking about it lol), that’s why I basically read that one first, then went back to the others till I could finally fully focus and fangirl over that one. YES, I have big problems haha<br />________<br /><br /><b>
  <u>ONE BY ONE RATINGS</u>
</b><br /><br />↣ Welcome to Shadowhunter Academy ★★★★.5/5<br />↣ The Lost Herondale ★★★.5/5<br />↣ The Whitechapel Fiend ★★★.5/5<br />↣ Nothing but Shadows ★★★/5<br />↣ The Evil We Love ★★★★/5<br />↣ Pale Kings and Princes ★★★★.5/5<br />↣ Bitter of Tongue ★★★.5/5<br />↣ The Fiery Trial ★★★.5/5<br />↣ Born to Endless Night ★★★★★/5 (this is worth the whole book, seriously. I was so pissed at myself because I wasn’t reading fast enough but at the same time I didn’t want it to end lol)<br />↣ Angels Twice Descending ★★★★★/5<br />________<br /><br /><b>
  <u>QUOTES</u>
</b><br /><br />“We can change ourselves, but never erase what we have been.” - Catarina<br />“You are who you have always been, and that is enough and more than enough.” - Jem<br />“To be a Shadowhunter was to live in the shadow of death.”<br />“Trust a faerie at your own risk, because they care for nothing but themselves. They sow nothing but destruction. And their preferred weapon is human love.”<br />“Fortunate are the ones who know the name of their heart. They are the ones whose hearts are never truly lost. They can always call their heart back home.” - Mark<br />“It’s yes, one day. For you, Alec, it’s always yes.” - Magnus<br />“You, Simon Lewis, couldn’t be a coward. Not if you tried. It’s not cowardly to make a choice about what you want your life to be. Choosing what’s right for you, maybe that’s the bravest thing you can do.” - Isabelle <br />_______<br /><br /><b>
  <u>FINAL THOUGHTS</u>
</b><br /><br />I loved this book. So many feels. Even if I liked some novellas more than others, they were all unique and every one added something to this world and characters that I love so much.<br />In some of them there were too many past scenes that made the novella slightly less interesting or exciting for my personal tastes. <br />During others, especially the last two, I was a mess of emotions. I was screaming, fangirling, sobbing and all those things that a very good book gives you!</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12632972859973123407"><b>edit, 2017</b>: I was going through my bookshelves while reorganizing them and I stumbled upon my physical copy of TFTSA. I read the e-novellas back to 2015 and then I got a free hardcover bind copy way later but never planned to re-read them. Not remembering basically anything about the short stories in it, I re-read them all today and<br/><i>jeez</i><br/>Was I disappointed.<br/>I remembered liking them quite a lot but re-reading them without any expectations made me feel a bit more crytical. I may say that I didn't lik</span>
  <span id="freeText12632972859973123407" style="display:none"><b>edit, 2017</b>: I was going through my bookshelves while reorganizing them and I stumbled upon my physical copy of TFTSA. I read the e-novellas back to 2015 and then I got a free hardcover bind copy way later but never planned to re-read them. Not remembering basically anything about the short stories in it, I re-read them all today and<br /><i>jeez</i><br />Was I disappointed.<br />I remembered liking them quite a lot but re-reading them without any expectations made me feel a bit more crytical. I may say that I didn't like at all the new secondary characters (and I felt pity just for <i>a certain one</i> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[George Lovelace <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> who dies for basically no reason but whatever, only two pages were spent on their death) and I was only happy to read about Simon regaining his memories back after two years but the rest... eh. <br />I didn't like the writing. Honestly, it annoyed the hell out of me. It was that kind of foolish-middle-grade-type-of-writing that I can't personally stand. If it weren't for the main characters from TMI - and the only one I didn't entirely appreciate was Isabelle, too out of character and too often <i>deus ex machina</i> -, I would have hated this collection. May I dare to suggest something to Cassandra Clare? <i>Please, don't co-write your own characters with other authors. Stop doing it. Don't let others move them but you. Don't write tons of novellas repeating always the same, damn stuff. Thanks.</i><br />Anyway, these are my new ratings:<br /><br /><b>1.</b> <i>Welcome to Shadowhunter Academy</i>: <b>2</b>/5 stars<br /><b>2.</b> <i>The Lost Herondale</i>: <b>2</b>/5 stars<br /><b>3.</b> <i>The Whitechapel Fiend</i>: <b>4</b>/5 stars<br /><b>4.</b> <i>Nothing But Shadows</i>: <b>3</b>/5 stars<br /><b>5.</b> <i>The Evil We Love</i>: <b>1</b>/5 stars<br /><b>6.</b> <i>Pale Kings and Princes</i>: <b>2</b>/5 stars<br /><b>7.</b> <i>Bitter of Tongue</i>: <b>3</b>/5 stars<br /><b>8.</b> <i>The Fiery Trial</i>: <b>2.5</b>/5 stars<br /><b>9.</b> <i>Born to Endless Night</i>: <b>3</b>/5 stars <br /><b>10.</b> <i>Angels Twice Descending</i>: <b>3.5</b>/5 stars<br /><br />Precisely, <b>2.6/5 stars</b>.<br />--------<br /><b>first review, 2015:</b><br /><b>1.</b> <i>Welcome to Shadowhunter Academy</i>: <b>3</b>/5 stars<br /><b>2.</b> <i>The Lost Herondale</i>: <b>4</b>/5 stars<br /><b>3.</b> <i>The Whitechapel Fiend</i>: <b>3.5</b>/5 stars<br /><b>4.</b> <i>Nothing But Shadows</i>: <b>5</b>/5 stars<br /><b>5.</b> <i>The Evil We Love</i>: <b>3</b>/5 stars<br /><b>6.</b> <i>Pale Kings and Princes</i>: <b>5</b>/5 stars<br /><b>7.</b> <i>Bitter of Tongue</i>: <b>4</b>/5 stars<br /><b>8.</b> <i>The Fiery Trial</i>: <b>4</b>/5 stars<br /><b>9.</b> <i>Born to Endless Night</i>: <b>4.75</b>/5 stars <br /><b>10.</b> <i>Angels Twice Descending</i>: <b>5</b>/5 stars<br /><br />In total, <b>4/5 stars</b>.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11576404524341759464">Holy god this book moved me, pleasantly surprised me, and completely unexpectedly destroyed me. I'm so mad I didn't read this early because I WAS TOTALLY MISSING OUT. I'll give the individual novellas ratings below, but I really believe this should be taken as a single work. <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[SIMON FREAKING LOVELACE STOLE MY HEART I CANNOT EVEN FREAKING DEAL WITH THIS. <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br/><br/>Ok I won't go super in-depth... but if you've read all the other Shadowhunter books YOU MUST READ THIS ONE WE GET T</span>
  <span id="freeText11576404524341759464" style="display:none">Holy god this book moved me, pleasantly surprised me, and completely unexpectedly destroyed me. I'm so mad I didn't read this early because I WAS TOTALLY MISSING OUT. I'll give the individual novellas ratings below, but I really believe this should be taken as a single work. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[SIMON FREAKING LOVELACE STOLE MY HEART I CANNOT EVEN FREAKING DEAL WITH THIS. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br />Ok I won't go super in-depth... but if you've read all the other Shadowhunter books YOU MUST READ THIS ONE WE GET TO SEE WILL AND TESSA, JAMES HERONDALE, THE CIRCLE, MAGNUS AND ALEC, LITERALLY EVERYONE IS IN THIS BOOK YALL YOU HAVE TO. <br /><br />It was freaking amazing I loved it so much. Minor spoilers ahead... I won't say anything major but from my language you might be able to guess some stuff so read at your own risk (: <br /><br /><b>*Welcome to Shadowhunter Academy:</b> <i>3.5/5 stars.</i> This one was by far the weakest... I also haven't read a Shadowhunter book in over a year, so getting back into it took a little bit.<br /><br /><b>*The Lost Herondale:</b> <i>4/5 stars.</i> Lol @Lady Midnight *winks*<br /><br /><b>*The Whitechapel Fiend:</b> <i>4/5 stars.</i> OMG JACK THE RIPPER YESSSSS! Still prefer Jem people imma just say that one again :P<br /><br /><b>*Nothing But Shadows:</b> <i> 5/5 FREAKING STARS!</i> This one was probably my favorite because OH MY LORDY JAMES HERONDALE MY PRECIOUS DARLING I CANNOT WAIT FOR THE LOST HOURS GIVE IT TO MEEEEEE! He's adorable and I know he gets real dark later on and I just wanna know whyyyyy and I cannot handle him I love him so much ahhhhh. <br /><br /><b>*The Evil We Love:</b> <i>5/5 stars.</i> HOLY VALENTINES CIRCLE. HOLY ROBERT LIGHTWOOD MAKING MISTAKES...<br /><br /><b>*Pale Kings and Princes:</b> <i>5/5 stars.</i> Simon and Izzy are goals like holy crap they are the CUTEST EVER SOMEONE SLAY ME. I also hope Helen comes to LA for LoS because I am livinggggg for her.<br /><br /><b>*Bitter of Tongue:</b> <i>5/5 stras.</i> MY PRECIOUS MARK OH MY GOD I CANNOT I WISH I READ THIS BEFORE LADY MIDNIGHT BECAUSE *sobs* I love mark he's so pure...<br /><br /><b>*The Fiery Trial:</b> <i>5/5 STARS!!</i> This may have been my second favorite. This was oh so sweet and I am just beyond happy for Clary and Simon. I saw this one coming but I wanted to cry when they were swimming toward each other like OMG MY BABIES <br /><br /><b>*Born To Endless Night:</b> <i>5/5 STARSSSS</i> Holy sweet God this was another one that made me just smile like an idiot. This even further cemented my love for Alec and Magnus and I just CANNOT HANDLE THE CUTENESS<br /><br /><b>*Angels Twice Descending:</b> <i>5/5 depressed stars</i> LMAO THIS WAS WHEN MY SOUL WAS RIPPED APART<br /><br />Anyway, needless to say, I am totally pumped for Lord of Shadows on Tuesday *squeals*</span>
  <a data-text-id="11576404524341759464" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2639236437" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2639236437" />
    <a title="Mariah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6728955-mariah"><img alt="Mariah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600089780p2/6728955.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2639236437?book_show_action=true">Dec 06, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mariah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mariah" href="/user/show/6728955-mariah">Mariah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6728955-mariah?shelf=tbr-2016-releases">tbr-2016-releases</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6728955-mariah?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6728955-mariah?shelf=mm">mm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6728955-mariah?shelf=own-hardcover">own-hardcover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6728955-mariah?shelf=series-shadowhunters">series-shadowhunters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6728955-mariah?shelf=read-in-2019">read-in-2019</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2639236437" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1673187308540996090">I’ve been staring at a wall for the past 40 minutes because I’m just- I can’t.<br/><a href='https://imgur.com/0VIptmk' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1575647890ra/28568900.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Alright, here’s the deal: some authors write short little anthologies, to – let me be blunt here – grab some coin. Because we’re all gonna buy them! But maybe not everyone will actually ever read them, but that’s beside the point. Cassandra Clare seems to refuse to do this. Instead she delivers this 700 page monster that will absolutely bite you – I’m pretty sure that’s where the tears came from!<br/><br/>This book features </span>
  <span id="freeText1673187308540996090" style="display:none">I’ve been staring at a wall for the past 40 minutes because I’m just- I can’t.<br><a href="https://imgur.com/0VIptmk" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1575647890ra/28568900.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Alright, here’s the deal: some authors write short little anthologies, to – let me be blunt here – grab some coin. Because we’re all gonna buy them! But maybe not everyone will actually ever read them, but that’s beside the point. Cassandra Clare seems to refuse to do this. Instead she delivers this 700 page monster that will absolutely bite you – I’m pretty sure that’s where the tears came from!<br><br>This book features a slew of old and beloved characters, as well as characters we’ve met before but hadn’t had a chance to get to know, and it also introduces brand new faces to join the wealth of Clare characters that will forever take up real estate in my heart.<br><br>To James, Matthew, Christopher &amp; Thomas – I will see you in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17699853.Chain_of_Gold__The_Last_Hours___1_" title="Chain of Gold (The Last Hours, #1) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener"> Chain Of Gold</a>, try not to blow anything up until then – you all know who I’m talking about.<br>To George, Jon, Julie, Beatriz and Marisol (<i>Bad Bunny voice</i>: LATINA GANG GANG) hoping to hear (good things only) about you in The Dark Artifices.<br><br>I was so floored by this. I’ve told this story so many times, but here it is again: I read the original TMI trilogy way back in 2009 and I kept buying the books (guilty as charged) but kept putting off reading until it became overwhelming to even think about catching up. This year I set out do just that, not only to reread the first three TMI books but to read all CC’s books before Chain of Gold comes out next year.<br><br>I’ve read over 43,000 pages so far this year (12/06/19) and 6.433 of those were Shadowhunter related. That’s 15% of my reading material. I am invested. I love this world. I love these characters. But it still surprised me how much of a visceral reaction I had to this.<br><br>It was actually very similar to how I felt while Reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16303287.The_Bane_Chronicles" title="The Bane Chronicles by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener"> The Bane Chronicles</a>. The Shadowhunters Chronicles can just be a world for you to get lost in, to leave your troubles behind. But it can be so much more than that if you are willing to look past the obvious. If you take a page from Clary’s book and strip away the paint of a glamour, to really see what is underneath. The lines Clare draws between Shadowhunters and Downworlders are much like the lines humans draw between each other because of race, religion, social status and wealth. It is a lesson that at our core, we are all the same. If you look closely enough you might just find that <i>all the stories are true</i>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1673187308540996090" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ublTqz1LbKrE8G51JnLejm2hJGMpssbTSeX1Vy5ZVRPjX2DFHFtqWzzErdh6Xt6xxdPlhED21OhpOl6pE4AiJQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('evdZF7N2K72JDsFz7pPs3YxvCZWksVcMQptuQHd0k9AgEWp5kmYtTHE6At6yv+ziJB3Ics31RTdiRMW+Sq3k5g==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('bookCover_17347389').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('bookCover_17347389').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_17347389').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>

  <span id="freeText3034768525788464205" style="display:none">Hello Goodreadsers. Here's my official bio:<br /><br />"Cassandra Clare was born overseas and spent her early years traveling around the world with her family and several trunks of fantasy books. Cassandra worked for several years as an entertainment journalist for the Hollywood Reporter before turning her attention to fiction. She is the author of City of Bones, the first book in the Mortal Instruments trilogy and a New York Times bestseller. Cassandra lives with her fiance and their two cats in Massachusetts."<br /><br />You can find me online at <br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.cassandraclare.com">www.cassandraclare.com</a><br /><br />I have a blog:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://cassandraclare.livejournal.com/">http://cassandraclare.livejournal.com/</a><br /><br />and a Facebook:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/Cassandraclare">http://www.facebook.com/Cassandraclare</a><br /><br />and a Twitter:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.twitter.com/cassieclare">www.twitter.com/cassieclare</a><br /><br />I'll be available here on Goodreads to answer questions for a Goodreads Author Discussion starting September 18 — <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/37113.Q_A_with_Cassandra_Clare">http://www.goodreads.com/group/show/3...</a><br /><br />Go sign up so you don't miss the conversation when it starts!</span>
